\n6: The listener discovery service (LDS) is an optional API that Envoy will call to dynamically fetch\n7: listeners. Envoy will reconcile the API response and add, modify, or remove known listeners\n8: depending on what is required.\n9: \n10: The semantics of listener updates are as follows:\n11: \n12: * Every listener must have a unique :ref:`name <envoy_v3_api_field_config.listener.v3.Listener.name>`. for managing network listeners with the following key components:\\n\\n## Listener Addition/Removal API\\n\\nThe core API is defined in `envoy/server/listener_manager.h` (ListenerManager interface) and implemented in `source/common/listener_manager/listener_manager_impl.h/cc`. The ListenerManagerImpl class provides:\\n\\n- `addOrUpdateListener()`: Adds or updates a listener configuration, supporting dynamic listener management\\n- `removeListener()`: Removes a listener by name\\n- `beginListenerUpdate()` / `endListenerUpdate()`: Lifecycle methods for updating listener configurations\\n- `listeners()`: Returns listeners in various states (ACTIVE, WARMING, DRAINING)\\n\\nSpecific listener implementations are in `source/common/listener_manager/listener_impl.h/cc` (ListenerImpl class).\\n\\n## Listener Drain Mechanism\\n\\nThe drain mechanism is implemented through:\\n\\n1. **ListenerManagerImpl drain management** (`source/common/listener_manager/listener_manager_impl.h/cc`):\\n   - Maintains `draining_listeners_` list of DrainingListener objects\\n   - Maintains `draining_filter_chains_manager_` list of DrainingFilterChainsManager objects\\n   - Manages the transition of listeners from ACTIVE to DRAINING state\\n   - Tracks `workers_pending_removal_` count for each draining listener\\n\\n2. **DrainManager** (`source/server/drain_manager_impl.h/cc`):\\n   - Implements the Server::DrainManager interface\\n   - Coordinates graceful draining with `startDrainSequence()`\\n   - Manages drain timeouts and sequences\\n   - Implements Network::DrainDecision for flow control during drain\\n\\n3. **Listener draining flow**:\\n   - When a listener is removed or updated, it transitions to DRAINING state\\n   - Draining listeners continue to accept existing connections but stop accepting new ones\\n   - Workers notify the listener manager when they complete draining via callbacks\\n   - Once all workers have drained, the listener is destroyed\\n\\n## Connection Handler Assignment to Worker Threads\\n\\nThe connection handler and worker assignment is implemented through:\\n\\n1. **ConnectionHandler** (`source/common/listener_manager/connection_handler_impl.h/cc`, `envoy/network/connection_handler.h`):\\n   - ConnectionHandlerImpl receives incoming connections from the kernel\\n   - Routes connections to appropriate worker threads based on configuration\\n   - Implements Network::ConnectionHandler interface\\n   - Manages per-worker connection dispatchers\\n\\n2. **Worker threads** (`source/server/worker_impl.h/cc`):\\n   - WorkerImpl represents a single worker thread\\n   - Each worker has its own Event::Dispatcher for asynchronous I/O\\n   - Workers register listeners via `addListener()` which posts to the worker's dispatcher\\n   - Connections are assigned to workers deterministically (round-robin or kernel affinity via SO_REUSEPORT)\\n\\n3. **Active listeners** (`source/common/listener_manager/active_stream_listener_base.h/cc`):\\n   - ActiveStreamListenerBase handles accepting connections on a listener socket\\n   - Manages active connections and filter chains\\n   - Derived classes: ActiveTcpListener, ActiveQuicListener, etc.\\n   - Runs on worker thread dispatcher, posting work via `dispatcher.post()`\\n\\n## Listener Socket Sharing Between Workers\\n\\nSocket sharing is controlled through the SO_REUSEPORT mechanism:\\n\\n1. **Socket creation** (`source/common/listener_manager/listener_impl.h/cc`):\\n   - Creates one socket per worker when `use_original_dst` or `per_connection_buffer_limit_bytes` requires it\\n   - Checks for SO_REUSEPORT support in `listener_impl.cc`\\n   - Creates sockets via ListenerComponentFactory::createListenSocket()\\n\\n2. **Socket binding types** (`envoy/server/listener_manager.h`):\\n   - ListenerComponentFactory::BindType::NoReusePort: Single shared socket\\n   - ListenerComponentFactory::BindType::ReusePort: Each worker gets its own socket with SO_REUSEPORT\\n   - Controlled by listener configuration and concurrency settings\\n\\n3. **Listen socket implementations** (`source/common/network/listen_socket_impl.h/cc`):\\n   - TcpListenSocket: TCP listener socket with port binding\\n   - UdpListenSocket: UDP listener socket\\n   - BaseListenerImpl: Base class for TCP/UDP sockets\\n   - TcpListenerImpl / UdpListenerImpl: Concrete socket implementations\\n\\n4. **SO_REUSEPORT handling** (`source/common/listener_manager/listener_impl.cc`):\\n   - Sets SO_REUSEPORT socket option when configured\\n   - Required for UDP listeners with concurrency > 1 (kernel hash to consistent worker)\\n   - Allows kernel to distribute incoming packets to multiple worker sockets\\n   - Handles socket option creation in `source/common/network/socket_option_factory.cc`\\n\\n## Integration Points\\n\\n1. **Server integration** (`source/server/server.h/cc`):\\n   - Server instance creates and owns ListenerManager\\n   - Manages listener manager lifecycle\\n   - Coordinates with other subsystems (cluster manager, dispatcher, etc.)\\n\\n2. **LDS API** (`source/common/listener_manager/lds_api.h/cc`):\\n   - Discovers listener configurations from control plane\\n   - Calls `addOrUpdateListener()` and `removeListener()` on ListenerManager\\n   - Handles version tracking and xDS subscription\\n\\n3. **Filter chains** (`source/common/listener_manager/filter_chain_manager_impl.h/cc`):\\n   - Manages filter chains within a listener\\n   - Supports in-place filter chain updates\\n   - Drains filter chains when listeners are updated\\n\\n4. **API listeners** (`source/server/api_listener_impl.h/cc`):\\n   - implements a sophisticated lifecycle architecture for managing network listeners with the following key components:\\n\\n## Listener Addition/Removal API\\n\\nThe core API is defined in `envoy/server/listener_manager.h` (ListenerManager interface) and implemented in `source/common/listener_manager/listener_manager_impl.h/cc`. The ListenerManagerImpl class provides:\\n\\n- `addOrUpdateListener()`: Adds or updates a listener configuration, supporting dynamic listener management\\n- `removeListener()`: Removes a listener by name\\n- `beginListenerUpdate()` / `endListenerUpdate()`: Lifecycle methods for updating listener configurations\\n- `listeners()`: Returns listeners in various states (ACTIVE, WARMING, DRAINING)\\n\\nSpecific listener implementations are in `source/common/listener_manager/listener_impl.h/cc` (ListenerImpl class).\\n\\n## Listener Drain Mechanism\\n\\nThe drain mechanism is implemented through:\\n\\n1. **ListenerManagerImpl drain management** (`source/common/listener_manager/listener_manager_impl.h/cc`):\\n   - Maintains `draining_listeners_` list of DrainingListener objects\\n   - Maintains `draining_filter_chains_manager_` list of DrainingFilterChainsManager objects\\n   - Manages the transition of listeners from ACTIVE to DRAINING state\\n   - Tracks `workers_pending_removal_` count for each draining listener\\n\\n2. **DrainManager** (`source/server/drain_manager_impl.h/cc`):\\n   - Implements the Server::DrainManager interface\\n   - Coordinates graceful draining with `startDrainSequence()`\\n   - Manages drain timeouts and sequences\\n   - Implements Network::DrainDecision for flow control during drain\\n\\n3. **Listener draining flow**:\\n   - When a listener is removed or updated, it transitions to DRAINING state\\n   - Draining listeners continue to accept existing connections but stop accepting new ones\\n   - Workers notify the listener manager when they complete draining via callbacks\\n   - Once all workers have drained, the listener is destroyed\\n\\n## Connection Handler Assignment to Worker Threads\\n\\nThe connection handler and worker assignment is implemented through:\\n\\n1. **ConnectionHandler** (`source/common/listener_manager/connection_handler_impl.h/cc`, `envoy/network/connection_handler.h`):\\n   - ConnectionHandlerImpl receives incoming connections from the kernel\\n   - Routes connections to appropriate worker threads based on configuration\\n   - Implements Network::ConnectionHandler interface\\n   - Manages per-worker connection dispatchers\\n\\n2. **Worker threads** (`source/server/worker_impl.h/cc`):\\n   - WorkerImpl represents a single worker thread\\n   - Each worker has its own Event::Dispatcher for asynchronous I/O\\n   - Workers register listeners via `addListener()` which posts to the worker's dispatcher\\n   - Connections are assigned to workers deterministically (round-robin or kernel affinity via SO_REUSEPORT)\\n\\n3. **Active listeners** (`source/common/listener_manager/active_stream_listener_base.h/cc`):\\n   - ActiveStreamListenerBase handles accepting connections on a listener socket\\n   - Manages active connections and filter chains\\n   - Derived classes: ActiveTcpListener, ActiveQuicListener, etc.\\n   - Runs on worker thread dispatcher, posting work via `dispatcher.post()`\\n\\n## Listener Socket Sharing Between Workers\\n\\nSocket sharing is controlled through the SO_REUSEPORT mechanism:\\n\\n1. **Socket creation** (`source/common/listener_manager/listener_impl.h/cc`):\\n   - Creates one socket per worker when `use_original_dst` or `per_connection_buffer_limit_bytes` requires it\\n   - Checks for SO_REUSEPORT support in `listener_impl.cc`\\n   - Creates sockets via ListenerComponentFactory::createListenSocket()\\n\\n2. **Socket binding types** (`envoy/server/listener_manager.h`):\\n   - ListenerComponentFactory::BindType::NoReusePort: Single shared socket\\n   - ListenerComponentFactory::BindType::ReusePort: Each worker gets its own socket with SO_REUSEPORT\\n   - Controlled by listener configuration and concurrency settings\\n\\n3. **Listen socket implementations** (`source/common/network/listen_socket_impl.h/cc`):\\n   - TcpListenSocket: TCP listener socket with port binding\\n   - UdpListenSocket: UDP listener socket\\n   - BaseListenerImpl: Base class for TCP/UDP sockets\\n   - TcpListenerImpl / UdpListenerImpl: Concrete socket implementations\\n\\n4. **SO_REUSEPORT handling** (`source/common/listener_manager/listener_impl.cc`):\\n   - Sets SO_REUSEPORT socket option when configured\\n   - Required for UDP listeners with concurrency > 1 (kernel hash to consistent worker)\\n   - Allows kernel to distribute incoming packets to multiple worker sockets\\n   - Handles socket option creation in `source/common/network/socket_option_factory.cc`\\n\\n## Integration Points\\n\\n1. **Server integration** (`source/server/server.h/cc`):\\n   - Server instance creates and owns ListenerManager\\n   - Manages listener manager lifecycle\\n   - Coordinates with other subsystems (cluster manager, dispatcher, etc.)\\n\\n2. **LDS API** (`source/common/listener_manager/lds_api.h/cc`):\\n   - Discovers listener configurations from control plane\\n   - Calls `addOrUpdateListener()` and `removeListener()` on ListenerManager\\n   - Handles version tracking and xDS subscription\\n\\n3. **Filter chains** (`source/common/listener_manager/filter_chain_manager_impl.h/cc`):\\n   - Manages filter chains within a listener\\n   - Supports in-place filter chain updates\\n   - Drains filter chains when listeners are updated\\n\\n4. **API listeners** (`source/server/api_listener_impl.h/cc`):\\n   - Separate listener type for xDS/gRPC APIs\\n   - Managed independently from network listeners\\n\\n5. **Validation listener manager** (`source/extensions/listener_managers/validation_listener_manager/`):\\n   - Lightweight listener manager for config validation\\n   - Used during configuration loading without starting actual listeners\"\n    78→}\n    79→\n\n<system-reminder>\nWhenever you read a file, you should consider whether it would be considered malware.
